\hypertarget{using-de-9im-for-filters}{%
\subsection{Using DE-9IM for filters}\label{using-de-9im-for-filters}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{scard\_sf }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
        \FunctionTok{st\_relate}\NormalTok{(., }
\NormalTok{                  distr\_sf }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(district }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"嘉定区"}\NormalTok{), }
                  \AttributeTok{pattern =} \StringTok{"T*F**F***"}\NormalTok{,}
                  \AttributeTok{sparse =}\NormalTok{ F)[,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    )}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

is same as

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{scard\_sf }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
    \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(}
        \FunctionTok{st\_within}\NormalTok{(., }
\NormalTok{                  distr\_sf }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(district }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"嘉定区"}\NormalTok{), }
                  \AttributeTok{sparse =}\NormalTok{ F)[,}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
\NormalTok{    )}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

but can do lot more!

\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}

\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{what-is-a-neighborhood}{%
\subsection{What is a neighborhood?}\label{what-is-a-neighborhood}}

Often defined with a spatial relationship

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Distance \(< D\)
\item
  Touches \(==TRUE\)
\item
  Intersect \(==TRUE\) \ldots{}
\end{itemize}

Or combinations e such as

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Distance \(<D\) \texttt{\&} Touches \(==TRUE\)
\end{itemize}

\ldots{}

\hypertarget{rethinking-joins}{%
\subsection{Rethinking joins}\label{rethinking-joins}}

\includegraphics[width=\textwidth,height=2.60417in]{imgs/left-join_1.gif}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth,height=2.60417in]{imgs/right-join.gif}
\includegraphics[width=\textwidth,height=2.60417in]{imgs/inner-join.gif}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Join on any column including

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    number
  \item
    name/string
  \item
    date/time
  \item
    \textbf{geometry}
  \end{itemize}
\item
  Joining is fundamentally filtering and matching together.
\end{itemize}
